Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 (Apollo 15-17 Command Module) program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Photography was by Ron Burkey, and transcription was performed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

024372,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
024373,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
024374,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Artemis (i.e., Colossus 3),
024375,000005:                                                                                                  ##              build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM)
024376,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for
024377,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo 15-17.
024378,000008:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
024379,000009:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Jim Lawton <jim DOT lawton AT gmail DOT com>
024380,000010:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
024381,000011:                                                                                                  ## Page Scans:  www.ibiblio.org/apollo/ScansForConversion/Artemis072/
024382,000012:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2010-01-26 JL   Started Artemis072 conversion based on Comanche055 
024383,000013:                                                                                                  ##                              module.
024384,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2010-01-31 JL   Finished Artemis072 conversion. Fixed build errors.
024385,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-01 JL   Fixed build errors.
024386,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-02 JL   Fixed page numbers. Removed duplicated code section
024387,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              on page 611.
024388,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-06 JL   Added missing "DEC 18" instruction. Added missing 
024389,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              code on page 618. Added missing line on page 601. 
024390,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              Fixed line 5 on p580, which is overprinted in the 
024391,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              scan. Fixed an EQUALS on p589. Removed spurious 
024392,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              PUSH on p598.
024393,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-13 JL   Fixed errors on pages 563, 589, 604, 619, 629.
024394,000024:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-20 RSB  Un-##'d this header.
024395,000025:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-05 RSB  Proofed comment text by diff'ing vs Comanche 55
024396,000026:                                                                                                  ##                              and corrected errors found, but only through about 
024397,000027:                                                                                                  ##                              p. 571 so far.  Note that while P20 is supposedly an 
024398,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              identical rev in the the two AGC versions, in fact
024399,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              the comments are rather  different, so that portion
024400,000030:                                                                                                  ##                              was proofed by traditional means, and the same is 
024401,000031:                                                                                                  ##                              true of a lesser degree to the  rest of it as well. 
024402,000032:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-06 RSB  Completed comment-text proofing. In the end, half or
024403,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              more of the file was proofed "traditionally", which
024404,000034:                                                                                                  ##                              has proven to be a pretty hit-and-miss process, so
024405,000035:                                                                                                  ##                              I'd judge that it probably needs still more proofing.
024406,000036:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-06 RSB  Re-proofed comment text using octopus/ProoferComments.
024407,000037:                                                                                                  ##                              The print- and/or scan-quality is so poor that it's 
024408,000038:                                                                                                  ##                              tough to feel much confidence in this method, but 
024409,000039:                                                                                                  ##                              combined with the manual proofing already-done, I 
024410,000040:                                                                                                  ##                              feel much more confident of the results now.
024411,000041:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-17 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified by 4-way diff'ing
024412,000042:                                                                                                  ##                              of Colossus 237 & 249, Comanche 55, and Artemis 72.

024415,000045: 
024416,000046:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
024417,000047:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
024418,000048:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -1
024419,000049:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
024420,000050: 
024421,000051:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024422,000052: 
024423,000053:                                                                                                  #  TO INITIALIZE THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION SUBROUTINES R22, R61CSM, AND
024424,000054:                                                                                                  #  R52, WHICH IN TURN CONTROL THE CSM ATTITUDE AND OPTICS POSITIONING,
024425,000055:                                                                                                  #  PROCESS BOTH OPTICS AND VHF TRACKING DATA, AND UPDATE EITHER THE LM
024426,000056:                                                                                                  #  OR THE CSM STATE VECTORS.
024427,000057: 
024428,000058:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024429,000059:                                                                                                  #    V37E20E
024430,000060: 
024431,000061:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024432,000062:                                                                                                  #    R22 (RENDEZVOUS TRACK DATA PROCESSING)
024433,000063:                                                                                                  #    R52 (AUTO OPTICS POSITIONING)
024434,000064:                                                                                                  #    R61CSM (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
024435,000065:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH            BANKCALL            UPFLAG
024436,000066:                                                                                                  #    DOWNFLAG           2PHSCHNG            LOADTIME
024437,000067:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           UPSTATE             INTPRET
024438,000068:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           MKRLEES             FINDVAC
024439,000069: 
024440,000070:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
024441,000071:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
024442,000072:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
024443,000073: 
024444,000074:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES
024445,000075:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024446,000076: 
024447,000077:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024448,000078:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024449,000079: 
024450,000080:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
024451,000081:                                                                                                  #    RNDVZFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG, TARG1FLG
024452,000082:                                                                                                  #    PRFTRKAT, V50N18FL
024453,000083: 
024454,000084: 36,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S7                                 
024455,000085: 36,2000                                           BANK                                           
024456,000086: 
024457,000087: 36,2016  E6,1774                                  EBANK=   R61CNTR                               
024458,000088: 36,2016                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
024459,000089: 
024460,000090: 36,2016           04636        PROG20             TC       BANKCALL                              
024461,000091: 36,2017           03731                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
024462,000092:                                                                                                  #  BLOCKING OF UPLINK IS DONE BY UPLINK PRG
024463,000093: 36,2020           31655                           CA       ADB                                   
024464,000094: 36,2021           55773                           TS       DBPTC

025184,000814: 
025185,000815:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R21)
025186,000816:                                                                                                  #  AND BACKUP SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R23)
025187,000817: 
025188,000818:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
025189,000819:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 1
025190,000820:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
025191,000821:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025192,000822: 
025193,000823:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM SIGHTING MARKS IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIG-
025194,000824:                                                                                                  #  ATION PROGRAM. CALLED BY ASTRONAUT VIA EXTENDED VERB
025195,000825:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
025196,000826:                                                                                                  #          R21 VIA V 57
025197,000827:                                                                                                  #          R23 VIA V 54
025198,000828:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
025199,000829:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
025200,000830:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      GOMARK2         GOMARKF
025201,000831:                                                                                                  #    INTPRET       GENTRAN         KLEENEX
025202,000832:                                                                                                  #    ENDMARK
025203,000833:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
025204,000834:                                                                                                  #    MARKRUPT USED BY SXTMARK HAS BEEN MODIFIED TO STORE MARK IN MRKBUF2
025205,000835:                                                                                                  #  FOR USE BY R22. WHEN ASTRONAUT IS FINISHED TAKING MARKS, HE HITS AN
025206,000836:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED ,   R21 IS TERMINATED THUS CAUSING THE FINAL MARK TO BE TRANSFRD
025207,000837:                                                                                                  #  TO MRKBUF2 FOR PROCESSING BY R22
025208,000838:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
025209,000839:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025210,000840:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
025211,000841:                                                                                                  #    7 REGISTER MRKBUF2 CONTAINING TIME2,TIME1,CDUY,OPTICS X,CDUZ, OPTICS Y,
025212,000842:                                                                                                  #  CDUX.
025213,000843:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025214,000844:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET AND RESET
025215,000845:                                                                                                  #    R21MARK   (COMMUNICATION TO MARKRUPT TO STORE MARKS IN MRKBUF1 + 2)
025216,000846:                                                                                                  #    R23FLG  INDICATES COAS MARKING
025217,000847:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025218,000848: 37,2263  E7,1722                                  EBANK=   MRKBUF1

025220,000850: 37,2000                                           BANK

025374,001004: 
025375,001005:                                                                                                  #   BVECTOR PERFORMS COMPUTATIONS FOR
025376,001006:                                                                                                  #  DELTAQ,THE MEASURED DEVIATION BASED ON THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE CSM-LE
025377,001007:                                                                                                  #  M STATE VECTOR ESTIMATES AND THE ACTUAL TRACKING MEASUREMENT.
025378,001008:                                                                                                  #  US,THE MODIFIED FICTITIOUS STAR DIRECTION VECTOR
025379,001009:                                                                                                  #  GEOMETRY VECTOR B ASSOCIATED WITH EACH TRACKING MEASUREMENT.
025380,001010:                                                                                                  #  INPUT
025381,001011:                                                                                                  #     UM,1/2 UNIT VECTOR ALONG THE CSM-LM LINE OF SIGHT (BASIC REF.SYSTEM)
025382,001012:                                                                                                  #     USTAR,FICTITIOUS STAR DIRECTION (1/2 UNIT VECTOR)
025383,001013:                                                                                                  #     RCLP,RELATIVE CSM TO LM POSITION VECTOR
025384,001014:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025385,001015:                                                                                                  #     USTAR,MODIFIED FICTITOUS STAR DIRECTION (1/2 UNIT VECTOR)
025386,001016:                                                                                                  #     BVECTOR = 9 DIMENSIONAL BVECTOR (1/2 UNIT VEC.)
025387,001017:                                                                                                  #     DELTAQ = MEASURED DEVIATION
025388,001018:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025389,001019:                                                                                                  #     L  CALL BVECTORS
025390,001020:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT
025391,001021:                                                                                                  #     L+1 OF CALLING SEQUENCE
025392,001022:

025459,001089: 
025460,001090:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING DATA PROCESSING ROUTINE (R22)
025461,001091: 
025462,001092:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025463,001093: 
025464,001094:                                                                                                  #  TO PROCESS RENDEZVOUS SIGHTING MARK AND VHF RANGING DATA TO UPDATE 
025465,001095:                                                                                                  #  THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER THE CSM OR LM AS DEFINED BY VEHUPFLG.
025466,001096:                                                                                                  #  (VEHUPFLG IS SET TO LM BY P20, CSM BY V81E, AND LM BY V80E.)
025467,001097: 
025468,001098:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025469,001099:                                                                                                  #    AUTOMATICALLY SELECTED BY P20
025470,001100: 
025471,001101:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025472,001102:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           INTPRET             GRP2PC
025473,001103:                                                                                                  #    GETUM              BVECTORS            INCORP1
025474,001104:                                                                                                  #    INCORP2            INTEGRV             PHASCHNG
025475,001105:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC              BANKCALL            GOTOV56
025476,001106:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           INSTALL             DOWNFLAG
025477,001107:                                                                                                  #    TRFAILOF           TRFAILON            TASKOVER
025478,001108:                                                                                                  #    POSTJUMP
025479,001109: 
025480,001110:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
025481,001111:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
025482,001112:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
025483,001113: 
025484,001114:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS OR ABORT EXIT MODES
025485,001115:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025486,001116: 
025487,001117:                                                                                                  #  INPUT
025488,001118:                                                                                                  #    MARK DATA, SEE R21 AND R23
025489,001119:                                                                                                  #    VHF RANGING DATA
025490,001120: 
025491,001121:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025492,001122:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT, NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025493,001123:                                                                                                  #    VHFCNT, NO OF VHF RANGING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025494,001124:                                                                                                  #    V06N49, EXCESSIVE UPDATE PARAMETERS-DELTA R AND DELTA V
025495,001125: 
025496,001126:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
025497,001127:                                                                                                  #    SOURCFLG, VINTFLAG, DIM0FLAG, INCORFLG, ORBWFLAG, RENDWFLG
025498,001128:                                                                                                  #    STATEFLG, D6OR9FLG, SKIPVHF, DMENFLG                                 AT THE INTERRUPTED DISPLAY.
025499,001129: 
025500,001130: 34,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S3

026225,001855: 
026226,001856: 04,3276           30071        TCQSTAL            CA       RUPTREG2                              
026227,001857: 04,3277           22002                           LXCH     Q                                     
026228,001858: 04,3300           52005                           DTCF                                           
026229,001859: 
026230,001860: 04,3301           00440        90MSCALR           OCT      440                                   #  90 MILLISEC IN SCALAR
026231,001861: 04,3302           77754        -DTSCALR           OCT      77754                                 #  -5.9375 MS IN SCALAR
026232,001862: 
026233,001863:                                                                                                  #  CRS61.1       4/10/68
026234,001864:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES

Page 593 

026236,001866:                                                                                                  #  OPTICS TRACKING OF THE LM AND LM TRACKING OF THE CSM RADAR TRANSPONDER
026237,001867:                                                                                                  #  AND TO COMPUTE THE &X-AXIS TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES
026238,001868:                                                                                                  #  COAS TRACKING OF THE LM.
026239,001869:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE SELECTED TRACKING ATTITUDE IF THE 
026240,001870:                                                                                                  #  MANEUVER IS LESS THAN 10 DEGREES BUT TO CALL R60 IF THE MANEUVER IS
026241,001871:                                                                                                  #  GREATER THAN 10 DEGREES OR IF THE R60FLAG IS SET.
026242,001872:                                                                                                  #           (1) EXTRAPOLATE LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS TO PRESENT TIME USING
026243,001873:                                                                                                  #               CONIC EQUATIONS.
026244,001874: 
026245,001875:                                                                                                  #           (2) CALCULATE LOS FROM CSM TO LM = RL - RC.
026246,001876: 
026247,001877:                                                                                                  #           (3) THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE IS DEFINED AS FOLLOWS:
026248,001878:                                                                                                  #               THE TRACK AXIS (I) IS ALIGNED ALONG THE LOS TO THE LM. THE
026249,001879:                                                                                                  #               TRACK AXIS (I) IS DEFINED AS:
026250,001880: 
026251,001881:                                                                                                  #               UNIT(I)=UNIT(Z  )COS55 &UNIT(X  )SIN55
026252,001882:                                                                                                  #                     -       -SC             -SC
026253,001883:                                                                                                  #           (4) COMPUTE DESIRED CDU ANGLES, USING VECPOINT.
026254,001884:                                                                                                  #           (7) FORM DIFFERENCE BETWEEN DESIRED AND ACTUAL CDUS.
026255,001885:                                                                                                  #               IF ANY OF THE THREE ANGLE DIFFERENCES EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES,
026256,001886:                                                                                                  #               GROSS MANEUVER IS REQUIRED. SIGNAL R61 (SET MPAC=1) TO
026257,001887:                                                                                                  #               OPERATE KALCMANU AND EXIT CRS61.1.
026258,001888:                                                                                                  #               IF ALL DIFFERENCES ARE LESS THAN 10 DEGREES, CONTINUE.
026259,001889: 
026260,001890:                                                                                                  #           (8) CALCULATE ORTHOGONAL LOS RATE IN REF COORDS AS
026261,001891: 
026262,001892:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATH = (UNITLOS(B1) X UNITDV(B1))(ABSDV(B7)/ABSLOS(B29))
026263,001893:                                                                                                  #               CONVERSION FACTOR OF 100/2PI (B4) REV CSEC PER RAD SEC IS
026264,001894:                                                                                                  #               APPLIED TO YIELD UNITS OF REVS/SEC. SCALE IS CARRIED AS
026265,001895:                                                                                                  #               B+1+1+7-29+4+1 PLUS RESULTS OF NORMALIZING ABSDV, ABSLOS.
026266,001896:                                                                                                  #               THE EXTRA B+1 RESULTS FROM RESCALING ABSDV B8 AFTER NORM
026267,001897:                                                                                                  #               TO AVOID OVFLOW ON DIVIDE.
026268,001898: 
026269,001899:                                                                                                  #               UNITLOS = UNIT( RL - RC) B1.
026270,001900:                                                                                                  #               UNITDY  = UNIT( VL - VC) B1.
026271,001901:                                                                                                  #               ABSLOS  = LENGTH OF LOS, METERS B29.
026272,001902:                                                                                                  #               ABSDV   = LENGTH OF DV , METERS/CSEC B7.
026273,001903: 
026274,001904:                                                                                                  #           (9) OBTAIN RATE IN SM COORDS.
026275,001905: 
026276,001906:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATHSM = (REFSMMAT)(OMEGATH).
026277,001907: 
026278,001908:                                                                                                  #           (10)OBTAIN GIMBAL ANGLE INCREMENTS FOR 0.1 SECOND.
026279,001909: 
026280,001910:                                                                                                  #               DTHETASM = (0.1)(OMEGATHSM)
026281,001911: 
026282,001912:                                                                                                  #           (11)OBTAIN DELCDUX,Y,Z USING SUBR SMCDURES.
026283,001913:                                                                                                  #               INPUT CONSISTS OF
026284,001914: 
026285,001915:                                                                                                  #               (A) VECTOR OF ANGULAR INCREMENTS, DTHETASM, STORED

Page 594 

026287,001917:                                                                                                  #                   IN V(DTHETASM).
026288,001918: 
026289,001919:                                                                                                  #               (B) SIN,COS CDUX,Y,Z FROM  SUBR CDUTRIG.
026290,001920: 
026291,001921:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OUTPUT OF SMCDURES FROM V(DCDU) TO VAC14D.
026292,001922: 
026293,001923:                                                                                                  #           (12)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN BODY(NB) COORDS USING SUBR SMNB.
026294,001924: 
026295,001925:                                                                                                  #               OMEGANB = (SMNB)(OMEGATHSM)
026296,001926: 
026297,001927:                                                                                                  #               SUBR SMNB REQUIRES  OMEGATHSM IN V(VAC32D) AND ACTUAL CDUS
026298,001928:                                                                                                  #               (Y,X,Z ORDER) IN V(VAC20D) WITH S1 OF VAC = BASE ADDRESS
026299,001929:                                                                                                  #               OF CDUS (FIXLOC + 20D).
026300,001930: 
026301,001931:                                                                                                  #           (13)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN CONTROL COORDS AS FOLLOWS
026302,001932: 
026303,001933:                                                                                                  #               WBODY = (MBDYTCTL)(OMEGANB)   UNITS=REVS/SEC(B0).
026304,001934: 
026305,001935:                                                                                                  #                              ( 0.5       0             0      ) BODY TO
026306,001936:                                                                                                  #               MBDYTCTL(B1) = (  0   COS(7.25)B1  -SIN(7.25)B1 )=CONTROL
026307,001937:                                                                                                  #                              (  0   SIN(7.25)B1   COS(7.25)B1 ) AXES
026308,001938:                                                                                                  #                                                                CONVERSION
026309,001939:                                                                                                  #                                                                 MATRIX
026310,001940: 
026311,001941:                                                                                                  #           (14)RESCALE WBODY TO UNITS OF 450 DEG/SEC BY APPLYING FACTOR
026312,001942:                                                                                                  #               OF 0.8 TO REVS/SEC.
026313,001943: 
026314,001944:                                                                                                  #           (15)ADDRESS LIVE AUTOPILOT REGISTERS IN BASIC (UNDER INHINT).
026315,001945: 
026316,001946:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DESIRED CDUS, SCALED 180 DEGREES, FROM T(SAVEDCDU)
026317,001947:                                                                                                  #               TO V(CDUXD).
026318,001948:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DELCDUS, SCALED 180 DEG, FROM V(VAC14D)
026319,001949:                                                                                                  #               TO V(DELCDUX).
026320,001950:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OMEGA CONTROL, SCALED 450 DEG/SEC, FROM V(MPAC)
026321,001951:                                                                                                  #               TO V(WBODY).
026322,001952:                                                                                                  #               RELINT, SET MPAC=0, EXIT CRS61.1
026323,001953: 
026324,001954:                                                                                                  #  CALL     L  CALL CRS61.1
026325,001955: 
026326,001956:                                                                                                  #  RETURNS  ALL TO L+1.
026327,001957: 
026328,001958:                                                                                                  #           (1) S(MPAC)=0. NORMAL EXIT. 3 SETS OF INPUTS FED TO DAP.
026329,001959:                                                                                                  #           (2) S(MPAC)=1. CALCULATED DESIRED CDUS,SP, SET IN T(CPHI)
026330,001960:                                                                                                  #               FOR KALCMANU. ABS(ACDU - DCDU) EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES.
026331,001961:                                                                                                  #           (3) S(MPAC)=2. GNCS AUTO MODE NOT SELECTED (BIT10=1).
026332,001962:                                                                                                  #           (4) S(MPAC)=3. DAP HOLD FLAG (HOLDFLAG) NOT EQUAL -1.
026333,001963: 
026334,001964:                                                                                                  #  INPUT    (1) TIME2,TIME1. COMPUTER CLOCK TIME,DP, CENTISEC B28.
026335,001965:                                                                                                  #           (2) CDUX,Y,Z. PRESENT CDU ANGLES,SP,2S COMPL HALF-REVS B0.
026336,001966:                                                                                                  #           (3) M(REFSMMAT),STABLE MEMBER COORDS B1.

Page 595 

026338,001968: 
026339,001969:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT   NORMAL. EXIT WITH S(MPAC) = 0.
026340,001970: 
026341,001971:                                                                                                  #           (1) CDUXD,CDUYD,CDUZD, DESIRED OUTER, INNER, MIDDLE CDU ANGLES,
026342,001972:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEGREES (HALF-REVS B0).
026343,001973:                                                                                                  #           (2) DELCDUX,DELCDUY,DELCDUZ. 0.1 SEC DCU ANGULAR INCREMENTS,
026344,001974:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEG.
026345,001975:                                                                                                  #           (3) WBODY,WBODY1,WBODY2. LOS ANGULAR RATE IN CONTROL COORDS,
026346,001976:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 450 DEG/SEC.
026347,001977: 
026348,001978:                                                                                                  #               SPECIAL. EXIT WITH S(MPAC) = 1.
026349,001979: 
026350,001980:                                                                                                  #           (1) CPHI,CTHETA,CPSI. DESIRED OUTER, INNER, MIDDLE CDU ANGLES,
026351,001981:                                                                                                  #               SP, 2S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEGREES.
026352,001982: 
026353,001983:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL SUBROUTINES USED   (B)=BASIC
026354,001984: 
026355,001985:                                                                                                  #           (1) CALCGA    (5) LOADTIME(B)  (9) SMNB
026356,001986:                                                                                                  #           (2) CDUTRIG   (6) MATMOVE
026357,001987:                                                                                                  #           (3) CSMCONIC  (7) RDCDUS(B)
026358,001988:                                                                                                  #           (4) LEMCONIC  (8) SMCDURES
026359,001989: 
026360,001990:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE (1) S(Q611),EBANK7  CRS61.1 EXIT .
026361,001991:                                                                                                  #           (2) S(Q6111)EBANK7  CALCDCDU EXIT.
026362,001992:                                                                                                  #           (3) T(SAVEDCDU) E6  SP VECTOR OF CDUDS.
026363,001993:                                                                                                  #           (4) V(SAVEPOS)  E7  CSM POS VEC AND  D(SAVEPOS)= LENGTH OF LOS.
026364,001994:                                                                                                  #           (5) V(SAVEVEL) E7  CSM VEL VEC.
026365,001995: 
026366,001996:                                                                                                  #  FLAGWDS  HOLDFLAG. USED, NOT SET.
026367,001997: 
026368,001998:                                                                                                  #  MISC     (1) ERASABLE ITEMP1 USED TO TEMP STORE EBANK UNDER INHINT.
026369,001999:                                                                                                  #           (2) ERASABLE P21TIME USED AS TEMP STORE DURING CRS61.1
026370,002000:                                                                                                  #           (3) ERAS DTHETASM USED AS TEMP STORE DURING EARLY CRS61.1
026371,002001:

Page 609 

026992,002622: 
026993,002623:                                                                                                  #  ..... S22.1 ORBITAL NAVIGATION ROUTINE
026994,002624:                                                                                                  #  MOD 1
026995,002625: 
026996,002626:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026997,002627:                                                                                                  #   1. UPDATE CSM STATE VECTOR
026998,002628:                                                                                                  #   2. UPDATE LANDMARK POSITION
026999,002629:                                                                                                  #   3. CONVERT W MATRIX FROM 9 TO 6 DIMENSIONS
027000,002630: 
027001,002631:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
027002,002632:                                                                                                  #   INTSTALL,INTEGRV,GETUM,SETRE,R-TO-TP,RP-TO-R,BVECTORS,INCORP1,INCORP2
027003,002633:                                                                                                  #   LALOTORV,S22F2410,LAT-LONG,ROWDOT
027004,002634: 
027005,002635:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION
027006,002636:                                                                                                  #   W=9X9 MATRIX
027007,002637:                                                                                                  #   ORBWFLAG=0 FOR INVALID W MATRIX,=1 FOR VALID W MATRIX
027008,002638:                                                                                                  #   ASTRONAUT ENTRY OF KNOWN,L,OFF
027009,002639:                                                                                                  #   8NN= NUMBER OF MARKS  DECIMAL INTEGER B-14
027010,002640:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT= TRANSFORMATION MATRIX
027011,002641:                                                                                                  #   MARKSTAT= ADDRESS OF START OF MARK DATA (MARK DATA OF EACH MARK IS
027012,002642:                                                                                                  #             STORED AS FOLLOWS,  TIME,AIG,SA,AMG,PA,AOG) TIME IS IN DOUBLE
027013,002643:                                                                                                  #             PRECISION,ALL OTHERS ARE IN SINGLE PRECISION
027014,002644:                                                                                                  #   CSM STATE VECTOR
027015,002645: 
027016,002646:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
027017,002647:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED CSM STATE VECTOR
027018,002648:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED LANDMARK POSITION
027019,002649:                                                                                                  #   NEW 6 DIMENSIONAL W MATRIX
027020,002650: 
027021,002651:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
027022,002652:                                                                                                  #   PUSH LIST,CSMPOS,ALPHAV,ERADM,UM,RCLP,USTAR,VARIANCE,X789,BVECTOR,8KK,
027023,002653:                                                                                                  #   S22LOC,SVMRKDAT TABLE,22SUBSCL,LANDMARK,CXOFF,S22C,LAT,LONG,ALT,
027024,002654:                                                                                                  #   TEMPOR1,S22TOFF,S221OFF,DSPTEM1,S22EORM,S22TPRIM
027025,002655: 
027026,002656: 30,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S6                                 
027027,002657: 30,2000                                           BANK

027749,003379: 
027750,003380:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINE NAME:   V89CALL
027751,003381:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO:  0                      DATE: 8 FEB 1968
027752,003382:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY:  DIGITAL DEVEL GROUP    LOG SECTION:  P20-P25
027753,003383: 
027754,003384:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
027755,003385: 
027756,003386:                                                                                                  #  CALLED BY VERB 89 ENTER DURING P00. PRIO 10 USED. CALCULATES AND
027757,003387:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS FINAL GIMBAL ANGLES TO POINT CSM +X AXIS OR PREFERRED AXIS
027758,003388:                                                                                                  #  (UNIT(Z)COS55 DEG + UNIT(X)SIN55 DEG) AT LM.
027759,003389: 
027760,003390:                                                                                                  #  1. KEY IN V 89 E ONLY IF IN PROG 00. IF NOT IN P00, OPERATOR ERROR AND
027761,003391:                                                                                                  #  EXIT R63, OTHERWISE CONTINUE.
027762,003392: 
027763,003393:                                                                                                  #  2. IF IN P00, DO IMU STATUS CHECK (R02BOTH). IF IMU ON AND ITS
027764,003394:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION KNOWN TO CGC, CONTINUE.
027765,003395: 
027766,003396:                                                                                                  #  3. FLASH DISPLAY V 04 N 06. R2 INDICATES WHICH SPACECRAFT AXIS IS TO
027767,003397:                                                                                                  #  BE POINTED AT LM.  INITIAL CHOICE IS PREFERRED AXIS. (R2=1).
027768,003398:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT CAN CHANGE TO (+X) AXIS (R2 NOT= 1) BY V22 E 2 E.  CONTINUE
027769,003399:                                                                                                  #  AFTER KEYING IN PROCEED.
027770,003400: 
027771,003401:                                                                                                  #  4. SET PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG ACCORDING TO OPTION DESIRED. SET FLAG
027772,003402:                                                                                                  #  FOR PREFERRED AXIS. RESET FLAG FOR X AXIS.
027773,003403: 
027774,003404:                                                                                                  #  5. CURRENT TIME IS STORED AND R63COMP IS CALLED
027775,003405: 
027776,003406:                                                                                                  #      R63COMP JOB:
027777,003407:                                                                                                  #        
027778,003408:                                                                                                  #        UPDATES CSM AND LM STATE VECTORS USING CONIC EQUATIONS
027779,003409: 
027780,003410:                                                                                                  #        CALCULATES BOTH PREFERRED AND X AXIS TRACKING ATT FROM 3SM TO LM.
027781,003411: 
027782,003412:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES AS INDICATED BY PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG
027783,003413:                                                                                                  #        ARE STORED FOR LATER R60CSM CALL.
027784,003414: 
027785,003415:                                                                                                  #  6. FLASH DISPLAY V 06 N18 AND AWAIT RESPONSE.
027786,003416: 
027787,003417:                                                                                                  #  7. RECYCLE- RETURN TO STEP 5.
027788,003418:                                                                                                  #     TERMINATE- EXIT R63 ROUTINE
027789,003419:                                                                                                  #     PROCEED- RESET 3AXISFLG AND CALL R60CSM FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
027790,003420: 
027791,003421: 
027792,003422:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: V 89 E
027793,003423: 
027794,003424:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED: CHKPOOH, R02BOTH, GOXDSPF, R63COMP, R60CSM
027795,003425: 
027796,003426:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS   1. OPERATOR ERROR IF NOT IN P00
027797,003427:                                                                                                  #           2. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU IS OFF
027798,003428:                                                                                                  #           3. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU ORIENTATION IS UNKNOWN

Page 626 

027800,003430: 
027801,003431:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: NONE
027802,003432: 
027803,003433:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  OPTION1, OPTION1+1, PRFTRKAT(PREF ATT FLAG),P21TIME, 3AXISFLG
027804,003434:

027862,003492: 
027863,003493:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME- P23 CISLUNAR MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION
027864,003494:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO
027865,003495:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY- TOM KNATT
027866,003496:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION- DO MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION BY INCORPORATION OF STAR 
027867,003497:                                                                                                  #  /EARTH AND STAR/MOON OPTICAL MEASUREMENTS.
027868,003498:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE- ASTRONAUT OPERATED
027869,003499:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED-R52,R53,R57,R60,ORBITAL INTEGRATION (INTEGRV)
027870,003500:                                                                                                  #  INCORP1,INCORP2,LALOTORV,LUNPOS  ,AND DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINES.
027871,003501:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES- VIA ROO
